on_actions = {
	#### PEACE/WAR VICTORY ON_CAPITULATION BLOCK ####
	#### PUT YOUR SHIT HERE
	# At the end of each global block, set the skip_default_capitulation GLOBAL flag
	# Otherwise shit will just get annexed
	# Really
	# It will.

	# FROM = winner
	# ROOT = country being capitulated/loser

	#See TNO_economy_scripted_effects regarding how transfer_GDP works
	on_capitulation = {
		effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: FROM: [From.GetName] ROOT: [Root.GetName] on_capitulation"

			set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
			FROM = {
				save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
			}
			ROOT = {
				save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
			}

			log = "[GetDateText]: winner/loser: FROM: [winning_country.GetName] ROOT: [losing_country.GetName] on_capitulation"

			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:losing_country = {
						any_allied_country = {
							has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = losing_country_multiple
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:winning_country = {
						any_allied_country = {
							has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
			}

			#Annexation block
			#This if block will only fire if FROM (capitulator) and ROOT (country being capitulated)
			#That is to say, if one side has completely lost (nobody left to fight on)
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						ROOT = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							any_other_country = {
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
								has_capitulated = no
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = war_won

				#Transfer 60% of every capitulated country's GDP to the winner
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							original_tag = ROOT
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						#transfer_GDP = yes
					}
				}
				#KOKSHETAU capitulates any nation
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							original_tag = KOK
						}
					}

					FROM = {
						white_peace = ROOT
						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = no
						}
						#khanate_update_reliance_unrest = yes
					}
					set_global_flag = skip_default_capitulation
				}

				#Indonesian civil war : FRI win
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							original_tag = FRI #free indo
						}

							original_tag = INS #normal indo
						}

							country_event = { id = USA_INS.02 }
						}	
					}
					else_if = { #USA not involved
						limit = {
							USA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_INS_CW_meddling } }
						}

							country_event = { id = USA_INS.04 }

									any_enemy_country = {
										OR = {
											is_central_siberian_nation = yes
											is_far_eastern_nation = yes
										}

									RKS = {
										check_variable = { num_owned_states > 9 }
									}
								}
							}
							GGR_Reload_main = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_war = no
								NOT = {
									any_country = {
										is_russian_nation = yes
										exists = yes
										NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
									}
								}
							}
							country_event = { id = goering_peace_events.13 }
							remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GGR_fall_rot }
						}
					}
					set_global_flag = skip_default_capitulation
				}
				#GÖRING ARC CAPITULATION
				if = {

								original_tag = GER

								is_russian_nation = yes
								is_central_asian_nation = yes

							is_in_faction = yes

					}
					ROOT = {

							limit = {
								has_country_flag = ARC_leader

							limit = {
								has_country_flag = ARC_leader

								has_country_flag = ARC_leader

								set_country_flag = ARC_leader

							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = no

				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = anti_heydrich_pact_formed

							OR = {
								original_tag = HGR
								# speidel bruh
								original_tag = GER
								original_tag = DSR
								original_tag = RNW
							}

						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = GGR
								original_tag = BGR
								original_tag = SGR
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						GER_GCW_off_a_fucker = yes
					}
					FROM = {
						white_peace = ROOT
						#message = gcw_capitulation_msg

						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = no

				# GCW 2 CAPITULATIONS
				#Goering defeats other contender nations
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = GGR_GCW2
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_war_with = GGR
								has_war_with = event_target:speidel_nation
								has_war_with = event_target:schorner_nation
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:schorner_nation
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:speidel_nation
								}
							}
							ROOT = {
								original_tag = GGR
							}
						}
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								is_in_faction_with = FROM
								has_country_flag = GCW2_faction_leader
							}
							country_event = { id = goering.2044 }
							annex_country = {
								target = GGR
								transfer_troops = no
							}

						limit = {
							FROM = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = GGR
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:speidel_nation

									original_tag = IRE

								}

							limit = {

							}
							random_country = {
								limit = {
									is_in_faction_with = FROM
									has_country_flag = GCW2_faction_leader
								}

								target = ROOT
								transfer_troops = no
							}

								clr_country_flag = GCW2_faction_leader
								clr_country_flag = GCW2_schorners_exile_nation
								clr_country_flag = GCW2_Schorner_nation

							random_country = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = GCW2_Schorner_nation
								}
								declare_war_on = {
									target = FROM
									type = annex_everything
								}
								country_event = { id = goering_GCW2.1 days = 0.04}
								FROM = {
									country_event = { id = goering_GCW2.2 days = 0.06}
								}
							}
							#if = {
							#	limit = {
							#		GGR = {

							#	}
							#	GGR = {

					#if = {
					#	limit = {

					#		FROM = {

					#		}
					#		ROOT = {
					#			#has_country_flag = GCW2_schorners_exile_nation
					#			#has_country_flag = GCW2_faction_leader
					#			has_country_flag = GCW2_Schorner_nation
					#		}

					#	GGR = {
					#		country_event = { id = goering.2046 }
					#	}

					#if = { # Non schorner nation gobbled up
					#	limit = {
					##		FROM = {

					#				is_in_faction_with = GGR
					#				original_tag = GGR
					#			}
					#		}

					#	annex_country = {
					#		target = ROOT
					#		transfer_troops = no

					if = { #Last schorner nation
						limit = {
							FROM = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = GGR
									original_tag = GGR
								}
							}
							ROOT = {
								original_tag = event_target:schorner_nation
							}
							NOT = {
								event_target:schorner_nation = {
									any_other_country = {
										is_in_faction_with = event_target:schorner_nation
									}
								}
							}
						}
						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = no
						
							}
						GGR = {
							country_event = { id = goering_GCW2.2 }
						}
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = GGR
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:schorner_nation
									original_tag = GRE
									original_tag = TUR
								}
							}
							ROOT = {
								event_target:speidel_nation = {
									original_tag = PREV
								}
							}

							annex_country = {

						#if = {

							limit = {

					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = FROM
						}
						every_state = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_claimed_by = PREV
									is_core_of = PREV
								}
								is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
							FROM = {
								transfer_state = PREV
							}

					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:schorner_nation
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:speidel_nation
									is_in_faction_with = GGR
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									FROM = {
										any_allied_country = {
											has_country_flag = GCW2_faction_leader
											any_owned_state = {
												is_core_of = PREV
												any_neighbor_state = {
													is_core_of = ROOT
												}
											}
										}
									}
									ROOT = {
										OR = {
											original_tag = SGR
											original_tag = RNW
											original_tag = OST
											original_tag = DST
											original_tag = BLR
										}

									NOT = {
										FROM = {
											any_allied_country = {
												any_owned_state = {
													is_core_of = PREV
													any_neighbor_state = {
														is_core_of = ROOT
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							random_country = {
								limit = {
									is_in_faction_with = FROM
									has_country_flag = GCW2_faction_leader
								}
								annex_country = {
									target = ROOT
									transfer_troops = no
								}
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								FROM = {
									any_owned_state = {
										is_core_of = PREV
										any_neighbor_state = {
											is_core_of = ROOT
										}
									}
									OR = {
										has_autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_reichskommissariat
										has_autonomy_state = autonomy_autonomous_reichskommissariat
									}
								}
							}
							annex_country = {
								target = ROOT
								transfer_troops = no
							}
						}
						else = {
							random_country = {
								limit = {
									any_owned_state = {
										is_core_of = PREV
										any_neighbor_state = {
											is_core_of = ROOT
										}
									}
									is_in_faction_with = FROM
								}
								annex_country = {
									target = ROOT
									transfer_troops = no
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = {
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										is_in_faction_with = event_target:schorner_nation
										is_in_faction_with = event_target:speidel_nation
										is_in_faction_with = GGR
									}
								}
							}
						}
						every_state = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_claimed_by = PREV
									is_core_of = PREV
								}
								is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
							FROM = {
								transfer_state = PREV
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										original_tag = GGR
										original_tag = SGR
										original_tag = RNW
									}
								}
							}
							every_country = {
								limit = {
									has_war_with = FROM
								}
								white_peace = FROM
							}
						}
						else = {
							ROOT = {
								GGR_GCW2_RK_collapse = yes
							}
						}
					}
					set_global_flag = skip_default_capitulation
				}
				#Capitulation block
				set_global_flag = war_continuing
			}
			clr_global_flag = skip_default_capitulation
		}
	}

			log="[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] declared war on [From.GetName]"
		}
